<name>Cheryl Hake< /name><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
Bargain World, is my new favorite thrift store!  I appreciate the many half off days, they offer, though regular prices are very reasonable.
Bargain World, offers a variety of items, including, men"s, women's and children's clothing, including plus sizes,  shoes for the whole family, as well as, accessories like, belts, purse‚Å∞s, scarves, etc.
There are a variety of househild items ; silverware and other utensils, glassware, decorative, knick knacks.
Electronic, learning toys, plush animals, baby items like  walkers, strollers, play litchens, play pens, baby bouncy seats, etc..  can be found, though inventory is changing, all the time.
There are waffle makers, coffee makers, electric skillets, crock pots, and more.
They carry  a minimal amount of furniture, wall art, and,  sporting goods.
In other words, Bargain World, has just about anything you're looking for.
Hopefully. you will find it as.much fun as I do.
Inventory changes, dsily. You never know what you'll find!< /text>

3 week update:
Clean gym, staff is professional, and the app makes for a smooth experience. The app tells me how crowded the gym is so i can plan accordingly, and the people are very nice and typically mind their own workouts.
Everyone cleans after themselves and there are always plenty of cleaning supplies to ensure the gym stays that way. The lockers here are better than at other places.                          Surprisingly, the showers are still open (limited-capacity, yet I have seen other gyms keep their showers closed), and the lockers feel like a luxury given the very low membership price.
The touchless membership sign-in is also helpful and offers a smooth experience at the entrance (wouldn't mind if it remained after the pandemic ends).
Worth the price.< /text>

If I could give negative stars, I would.  I've lived in some dumps and don't get me wrong, the apartment itself is lovely, if not overpriced... but this is the worst living experience I have ever had.

Here are some of the amenities you will get when you move in!

1) Vermin! So much vermin. There will be roaches, there will be mice, and there will be no one to really care about it.  In fact, if you call your manager and they schedule a pest control person, you will likely not be consulted as to the time they arrive or they might schedule them to go to the wrong apartment altogether.

2) People walking in and out of your apartment with or without notice!  I got the 24 hour notice before my manager or someone else entered my unit maybe once in the year I was a tenant at an Afton Properties building.  As I mentioned, pest control just had open access to my unit, it seemed, regardless of my requests or preferences.  My manager also on 2 occasions entered my unit despite my objections with an hour notice once and a refusal to find a different time when I could have someone else in the unit another.  Neither instances were emergencies nor were they unavoidable.

3) Managers who just don't care.  We went through three or four in my year at the apartment.  The first is the one who refused to help with the bees until after 10A.  The second took over a day to get back to me about the roaches. But the fourth repeatedly told me and other tenants that she wouldn't be helping us with our issue, or at least not the way we needed.  She entered my apt w/o proper notice, she never showed any interest in working with my schedule.  When I did finally figure out a way to request to go into work late since she refused to do the walkthrough an hour earlier so that I could get to work on time, she was 20min late and didn't send me any sort of text or call to let me know that she would be. I have never felt more disrespected or like I was demanding the moon because I didn't want strangers traipsing around in my apartment without my being there than I did when speaking with this woman.

4) Strangers who wander the halls and knock on apartment doors at 5AM and managers who don't report the need to fix the main entrances to prevent this from happening again!  True story.  There was a dude wandering around the halls in our apartment building who knocked on my door before going to my friend's door when I didn't answer.  We told our manager, he told us to file a report with the police who couldn't do anything. But no, a month later I had people from the management company in my apartment, told them about the incident, and it was clearly the first they'd heard about it.  Still didn't fix or update any of the locks though.

which brings me to...

< Review>
I was looking for an apple car play stereo for my 2014 Honda Civic. As I did my search and read my reviews I noticed this place called Sound Scape in Downey, CA.

When I called the first time and spoke with John he provided the most honest, genuine, customer service, and patience attitude towards me when it came to asking 100 questions on the product, pricing, and financial options he provided. Not once did he come off as a pushy sale guy and not once did he try to sell me things I did not need, which to me is a major plus because some places I went to see and called would try so hard to get me to upgrade things I didn't need to upgrade.

I called a few more times before making my appointment with John and sound scape and each time he was just an overall, honest and genuine person and after my third time calling I just decided to go with him and make my appointment for this Saturday 2/22/2020.  He gave me reassurance that the product had a one year warranty and he gave me reassurance about his life time warranty on his installation, that made me so happy.

Keep in mind I know nothing about cars except for what I research and even then its a scary situation when it comes to people installing things into your car. I love that they took their time when it came to installations and I love that John took the time to really show me how to work with my product. I love that they didn't leave a bunch of wires sticking around and I loved that in the end I am enjoying my new apple car play.

Overall, if you are looking for a new audio system for your car Sound Scape and John is the best place to go too and I would totally recommend this place to anyone I know that is looking to upgrade their cars. Thank you John for being a very honest, genuine, and patient man towards people like me who ask a lot of questions and have a lot of doubts about things. You make things very easy and very welcoming.</Review>

< Text>
I ordered a component speaker install through Amazon.

At first, I didn't get contact back within 1 business day (which is what was written on the Amazon page), so on the 2nd day I decided to stop by in person. When I arrived, I spoke with John, who told me that he called me just a little while ago. Sure enough, John called me while I was driving (though I was unable to pick up the call at the wheel) - I just didn't know whose number it was at the time.

I drove to Downey from Irvine, and John was very accommodating. He said that as soon he was done working on an install for the car he was working on, which he estimated would be roughly 45 minutes, he'd install the speakers into my car and call me once it was done. Never having set foot in Downey, he also directed me to the local mall to have a fun time in the meantime. From the time that I left the building, to the time that I came back after his call, a little over 2 hours went by - including the 45 minutes that weren't related to the install I purchased, leaving roughly 1:15 to 1:30 involving the work on my car. I was pleasantly surprised!

When I got back, John was very helpful in explaining all the aspects behind my new speakers vs. my old ones, and demonstrated that he was very knowledgeable with the expert advice he related to me when I asked him about a stereo and an amplifier and what effect it would have on my sound quality. At no point during any of our interactions did I feel like I was being pressured to purchase any product or additional service. John was straightforward, prompt, and extremely helpful (along with having a wonderfully friendly and cheery character).

Best Buy's installation bay had quoted me $100 for EACH pair of speakers, on top of a material fee and the costs of harnesses, for a total of roughly $235-240. Geez! SoundScape charged a flat $100 component installation for BOTH the front and rear pairs of speakers! The new speakers sound absolutely fantastic and I can't see anything at all indicating that work had been done on my car.

I recommend this shop to anyone who wants quality service from knowledgeable staff at great prices. SoundScape and John have equally earned my business, and I will gladly be driving all the way up to Downey every time I need help with anything car audio. A+++++</Text>

<review>One of my favorite places for lunch. Pizza by the slice, the size of a medium pizza at most places. I usually go for the daily special. $8 for 2 slices and 3 toppings and a can of soda. Put in perspective, a slice of pepperoni is $4.50 and 2 toppings is $5. Again for the price, the size is enough for a few people. It's also a thin crust pizza. Certain times of the day, lunch, can get real busy and can take anywhere between 8-20 min to get your slice. You can try calling the order in before hand, I have done this a few times. He may not always answer because of working alone usually, but you can keep trying.

On a side note, if you do want to try it out, the best bet would be on a slower day through the week (Monday-Friday, have not gone during the weekend) would be on Wednesday. During this time is the farmers Market and he gets less foot traffic around his area.<//review>< user_id>

<user_name>Nely L√≥pez</user_name><user>102803704524739116517<//user><time>1619396384011</time><Pics>None< /Pics><review>Always an excellent customer experience.</review><resp>None< /resp>< gmapID>

<Date>1600973788206</Date><gmap_id>0x809050178d00c439:0x5dd3e975c6f80406<//gmap_id>< review>
Same review applies to almost every In-N-Out I've been to. That's consistency.

Great customer service as usual. I always find it amazing how a place like McDonald's will have a young crew like In-N-Out but everyone there looks and acts like they would rather be anywhere else. At least at In-N-Out things are a bit more rosy. I was visiting the area and having an In-N-Out like the ones back home is always a pleasure. Nothing beats this place or comes close. Forget McDonald's, Wendy's, whatever other mediocre fast food joint is out there. If you've never heard of In-N-Out or never had it, sorry East Coasters, you have to try this place whenever you're in Arizona or California. There really is no excuse.

The wait time was not bad. I went through the drive-thru and they were pretty fast and efficient. I think I waited about 10 minutes total from entering the line and getting my food, so not too bad at all. A lot of In-N-Outs are clogged to heck with their drive-thrus. Maybe I visited at the right time. Maybe people are eating out less now. Looking at the line behind me I think that might not really be the case.

I will say this one more time. If you have never had In-N-Out, go now!! Only excuse is if you're in a state that doesn't have it and are reading this long review for some strange reason.</review>

My favorite place to get a fast food burger. Definitely go for animal style if you haven't already. Their food is always fresh and the small selection means quality ingredients.
